
# REST API JSON Payload Documentation

## GET /api/invoices - Retrieve Invoice List

### Request Payload (Query Parameters)
```json
{
  "pageNumber": 1,
  "pageSize": 10,
  "sortBy": "issueDate",
  "sortDirection": "desc",
  "filters": {
    "companyIds": ["10469762", "10486148"],
    "statuses": ["Overdue", "Paid", "Pending", "Draft"],
    "dateRange": {
      "issueDateFrom": "2018-01-01",
      "issueDateTo": "2025-12-31",
      "dueDateFrom": "2019-01-01",
      "dueDateTo": "2025-12-31"
    },
    "amountRange": {
      "minAmount": 1000.00,
      "maxAmount": 100000.00,
      "currency": "USD"
    },
    "reportingCountries": ["US", "GB", "IT"],
    "projectNumbers": ["PRJC-581396-2018-SCM-USA"],
    "searchTerm": "Kerry"
  }
}
```

### Error Response Payload
```json
{
  "data": null,
  "isSuccess": false,
  "message": "Invalid date range provided",
  "errorCode": "INVALID_DATE_RANGE"
}
```

## POST /api/invoices - Create New Invoice

### Request Payload
```json
{
  "companyId": "10469762",
  "projectNumber": "PRJC-581396-2018-SCM-USA",
  "contractId": 15872,
  "serviceIds": [1184, 1616],
  "invoiceNumber": "INV-2025-001",
  "referenceNumber": "REF-2025-001",
  "amount": 25000.00,
  "currency": "USD",
  "issueDate": "2025-09-19",
  "dueDate": "2025-10-19",
  "paymentTerms": "Net 30",
  "description": "ISO 9001:2015 Initial Certification",
  "lineItems": [
    {
      "description": "Initial Audit - Stage 1",
      "quantity": 2,
      "unitPrice": 5000.00,
      "totalPrice": 10000.00
    },
    {
      "description": "Initial Audit - Stage 2",
      "quantity": 3,
      "unitPrice": 5000.00,
      "totalPrice": 15000.00
    }
  ],
  "taxRate": 0.10,
  "taxAmount": 2500.00,
  "totalAmount": 27500.00,
  "createdBy": 15
}
```

# Original GraphQL Documentation

-------
{"operationName":"GetInvoiceList","variables":{},"query":"query GetInvoiceList {\n  InvoiceListPage {\n    data {\n      items {\n        amount\n        billingAddress\n        company\n        contactPerson\n        dueDate\n        invoice\n        issueDate\n        originalInvoice\n        plannedPaymentDate\n        referenceNumber\n        status\n        reportingCountry\n        projectNumber\n        accountDNVId\n        __typename\n      }\n      __typename\n    }\n    isSuccess\n    message\n    errorCode\n    __typename\n  }\n}"}
